Who's ready for a delicious #brunch ??? Head over to  the raymond 1886 off of Fair Oaks in Pasadena . I had their style of a breakfast tostada with some potatoes and my wife had the Italian baked eggs. We even shared the homemade cinnamon roll. This was really good and surprisingly filling. Here's a tip so you don't wait !!! Sit at the BAR, they have a full menu there. We really enjoy the ambiance and the food here. Get here early cause parking can be difficult here.</review>

<UserId.>109013947771483713211< /UserId.><user_name>Michael Han<//user_name><date>1542487321415</date><rate>4<//rate>< Text>
Came on a Friday night for a birthday dinner, party of 15. Sat outside; it was a bit cold but they have heat lamps. The outside area isn't that big. The restaurant is kind of hidden; you need to look for the sign. If turning left from the street in front, it comes up to you really quick after the turn; take the first driveway. They offer valet for $6. The food was good; service was slow but we had a large party. They seemed to be short staffed since the bus boy starter taking our orders; our waitress completed taking our orders. The bread and house made butter were good. I had the New York steak with potatoes, which was also good. The steak is cut for you and made as ordered (mine was medium). The fries (skinny fries) and house made ketchup were good as well. The old fashioned was made well; not too strong or sweet. Overall, not too expensive but wasn't cheap; worth it to go.<//Text>

March 5th, 2021  ANNOUNCEMENT

We are now back to ONE Jumma Salah and we offer both indoor outdoor accomodations by the grace of Allah . But we are strictly following the COVID 19 guidelines of maintaining 6ft distancing and mask wearing. Our Jumma khutba starts at 1:10pm followed by prayer at 1:30pm.
We are encouraging sisters to perform their prayers at home  at the moment due to lack of space at the masjid.

Apart from Friday Jumma, we are also open for 5 times prayers.

Please make sure to follow all Covid 19 related guidelines , Masks are mandatory,  bring your own Prayer rug, social distancing,  perform Wadu at home, no chit chat after Salah
Jazak Allah for your understanding and cooperation.
_--++++++++++++++++++++++
Ramadan Announcement:

Due to the ongoing Covid 19 Pandemic situation ICNOHO Ramadan programming will be as follows:

1. THERE WILL BE NO IFTAR                      PROGRAM
2. Masjid will have Dates ,   fruit and drink available for Iftar for any one stopping by for Maghrib Salah.
3.Traweeh will be conducted (20 Rakah) during the month. It will be shorter version than normal.
4. All Covid related CDC guidelines will be followed...social distancing,  Mask should be worn, Bring your own Prayer rug etc.
5. At present we are recommending women should not attend. We will further review this matter during Ramadan.

6. Itteqaf during the last 10 days of Ramadan will be allowed to only 3 individuals. Please request early if you want to do so.
May Allah Subanaho Tala
guide us to fulfill our obligations during the month of Ramadan.  Aameen.

I place my order through the app, pay with my reloadable card, earn points for free items, and by the time I walk in my order is ready at pickup for me. <user_id>111280814163699935749< /user_id><user_name>Ileana Contreras< /user_name><Resp>None</Resp><Rate>3< /Rate>< review>
It's a great location to nab some coffee during my work shift. Unfortunately each time I've visited to pick up a mobile order, I've always been put last on priority. Every time I come in and ask whether they've received my mobile order, they just become aware of it and put me behind the queue after everyone else who was in line. I had spent my whole lunch break waiting for my drink!

Beside that, there are a handful of exceptional baristas that have made my visit barable and made me attempt to revisit the store several times over. Not all of them are as approachable, but I understand the grueling hours of working in a busy store. Some seem to still be learning even, and it's because of all that that I have to give them a pass.

But I don't think I'll be returning to this one again anytime soon. Unless I have time to spare for the extra 20 minutes it takes to make a tall macchiato.</review>
